## Translation Methodology

This translation employs a **three-layer decipherment approach**:

### Layer 1: Prakrit Phonetic Base
Medieval Indic consonant-vowel patterns provide the phonetic foundation.
Cognative pre-forms from pre-forms.json provide consciousness/ritual terminology.

### Layer 2: Tamil-Siddha Technical Terminology
Medical and alchemical terms from South Indian Siddha medicine traditions.
Cross-validated with tamil_lexicon.json.

### Layer 3: European Cipher Overlay
Latin abbreviations and Germanic/Italian linguistic adaptations.
Cross-validated with latin_lexicon.json (101,545 entries).

### Cipher Rules Applied (Phases 8, 13, 14, 19, 20):
- **-aiin suffix**: Botanical medicine nominalizer (daiin = root medicine)
- **-saiin/-raiin**: Extended botanical suffixes (stem/resin medicine)
- **-edy/-eedy suffix**: Process verbs (shedy = prepared, chedy = extracted)
- **-dy suffix**: Simple completion marker
- **qo- prefix**: Volatile/celestial/dual (qokeedy = mercury/distilled)
- **o- prefix**: Plant/organic (otaiin = leaf, okaiin = flower)
- **ch-/sh- prefix**: Process/state markers
- **-ain suffix**: Quality descriptors (sain = hot, tain = cold)
- **-ol suffix**: Purpose or powder (chol = powder, shol = purified)
- **-ky suffix**: Celestial/like quality

---

## Section Organization

The manuscript is organized into distinct sections:

1. **Botanical Section** (f1r - f49v): Herbal medicine, plant identification
2. **Astronomical Section** (f50r - f74v): Medical astrology, timing
3. **Biological Section** (f75r - f89v): Hydrotherapy, baths, reproduction
4. **Pharmaceutical Section** (f90r+): Recipes, formulations, preparations
